           Please provide a plan that achieves the goal from the initial state.

Model:     The scene describes several objects (`v8`, `v12`, `v14`, `v16`, `v18`) that need to be placed on the `v20` surface. The robot has two arms, `v4` and `v6`, both of which are currently empty. Several poses are defined for each object, some of which are current (`atpose`), and some of which are potential placements or grasps. A large number of base configurations (`q` objects) and trajectories (`t` objects) are also defined, along with their corresponding kinematic information (`kin`) and base motion information (`basemotion`). The `v20` object is indicated as a stackable surface for objects `v8`, `v12`, `v14`, `v16`, and `v18`.
           
           The goal is to have all five objects (`v8`, `v12`, `v14`, `v16`, `v18`) on the `v20` surface.
           Currently, `v8` is at `v9` (on `v11`), `v12` is at `v13` (on `v11`), `v14` is at `v15` (on `v11`), and `v18` is at `v19` (on `v11`), and `v16` is at `v17` (on `v11`).
